root/sysdeps/x86_64/fpu/multiarch/svml_d_tan4_core_avx2.S

  17    https://www.gnu.org/licenses/.  */
  18 
  19 /*
  20  * ALGORITHM DESCRIPTION:
  21  *
  22  *      1) Range reduction to [-Pi/4; +Pi/4] interval
  23  *       a) Grab sign from source argument and save it.
  24  *       b) Remove sign using AND 0x7fffffffffffffff operation
  25  *       c) Getting octant Y by 2/Pi multiplication
  26  *       d) Add "Right Shifter" (0x4330000000000000) value
  27  *       e) Treat obtained value as integer for destination sign setting.
  28  *          Shift first bit of this value to the last (sign) position (S << 63)
  29  *       f) Change destination sign if source sign is negative
  30  *          using XOR operation.
  31  *       g) Subtract "Right Shifter" (0x4330000000000000) value
  32  *       h) Subtract Y*(PI/2) from X argument, where PI/2 divided to 4 parts:
  33  *          X = X - Y*PI1 - Y*PI2 - Y*PI3 - Y*PI4;
  34  *      2) Rational polynomial approximation ( at [-Pi/4; +Pi/4] interval)
  35  *       a) Calculate X^2 = X * X
  36  *       b) Calculate 2 polynomials:
  37  *          P = X * (P0 + X^2 * (P1 + x^2 * (P2 + x^2 * (P3))));
  38  *          Q = Q0 + X^2 * (Q1 + x^2 * (Q2 + x^2 * (Q3)));
  39  *       c) Swap P and Q if first bit of obtained value after
  40  *          Right Shifting is set to 1. Using And, Andnot & Or operations.
  41  *       d) Divide R = P / Q;
  42  *      3) Destination sign setting
  43  *       a) Set shifted destination sign using XOR operation:
  44  *          R = XOR( R, S );
  45  *
  46  */
  47 
  48 /* Offsets for data table __svml_dtan_data_internal
  49  */
  50 #define _dAbsMask                       0
  51 #define _dRangeVal                      32
  52 #define _dRShift                        64
  53 #define _dCoeffs                        96
  54 #define _dReductionRangeVal             26720
  55 #define _dInvPi                         26752
  56 #define _dPI1                           26784
  57 #define _dPI2                           26816
  58 #define _dPI3                           26848
  59 #define _dPI1_FMA                       26880
  60 #define _dPI2_FMA                       26912
  61 #define _dPI3_FMA                       26944
  62 #define _dP1                            26976
  63 #define _dP2                            27008
  64 #define _dP3                            27040
  65 #define _dQ0                            27072
  66 #define _dQ1                            27104
  67 #define _dQ2                            27136
  68 #define _dQ3                            27168
  69 
  70 #include <sysdep.h>
  71 
  72         .text
  73     .section .text.avx2,"ax",@progbits
  74 ENTRY(_ZGVdN4v_tan_avx2)
  75         pushq     %rbp
  76         cfi_def_cfa_offset(16)
  77         movq      %rsp, %rbp
  78         cfi_def_cfa(6, 16)
  79         cfi_offset(6, -16)
  80         andq      $-32, %rsp
  81         subq      $96, %rsp
  82 
  83 /* Legacy Code */
  84         xorl      %r9d, %r9d
  85         vmovupd   _dAbsMask+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm14
  86         vmovupd   _dRShift+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm2
  87         vmovupd   _dInvPi+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm6
  88         vmovupd   _dPI1_FMA+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm3
  89         vmovupd   _dP3+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm9
  90         vmovapd   %ymm0, %ymm15
  91 
  92 /* b) Remove sign using AND 0x7fffffffffffffff operation */
  93         vandpd    %ymm14, %ymm15, %ymm1
  94 
  95 /*
  96  * c) Getting octant Y by 2/Pi multiplication
  97  * d) Add "Right Shifter" (0x4330000000000000) value
  98  */
  99         vfmadd213pd %ymm2, %ymm1, %ymm6
 100 
 101 /* g) Subtract "Right Shifter" (0x4330000000000000) value */
 102         vsubpd    %ymm2, %ymm6, %ymm11
 103         vpsllq    $62, %ymm6, %ymm7
 104 
 105 /*
 106  * e) Treat obtained value as integer for destination sign setting.
 107  * Shift first bit of this value to the last (sign) position (S << 63)
 108  * f) Change destination sign if source sign is negative
 109  * using XOR operation.
 110  */
 111         vpsllq    $63, %ymm6, %ymm4
 112 
 113 /* X = X - Y*PI1 - Y*PI2 - Y*PI3 - Y*PI4; */
 114         vfnmadd213pd %ymm1, %ymm11, %ymm3
 115         vfnmadd231pd _dPI2_FMA+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm11, %ymm3
 116         vfnmadd132pd _dPI3_FMA+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm3, %ymm11
 117         vmovupd   _dQ3+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm3
 118 
 119 /* a) Calculate X^2 = X * X */
 120         vmulpd    %ymm11, %ymm11, %ymm10
 121 
 122 /*
 123  * b) Calculate 2 polynomials:
 124  * P = X * (P0 + X^2 * (P1 + x^2 * (P2 + x^2 * (P3))));
 125  * Q = Q0 + X^2 * (Q1 + x^2 * (Q2 + x^2 * (Q3)));
 126  * Assume P0 = 1
 127  */
 128         vfmadd213pd _dP2+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm9
 129         vfmadd213pd _dQ2+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm3
 130         vfmadd213pd _dP1+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm9
 131         vfmadd213pd _dQ1+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm3
 132         vmulpd    %ymm9, %ymm10, %ymm9
 133         vfmadd213pd _dQ0+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm3
 134         vfmadd213pd %ymm11, %ymm11, %ymm9
 135 
 136 /* 1) Range reduction to [-Pi/4; +Pi/4] interval */
 137         vxorpd    %ymm8, %ymm8, %ymm8
 138         vcmpneqpd %ymm8, %ymm7, %ymm2
 139 
 140 /* a) Grab sign from source argument and save it. */
 141         vandnpd   %ymm15, %ymm14, %ymm5
 142         vxorpd    %ymm5, %ymm4, %ymm0
 143 
 144 /*
 145  * c) Swap P and Q if first bit of obtained value after
 146  * Right Shifting is set to 1. Using And, Andnot & Or operations.
 147  */
 148         vandnpd   %ymm9, %ymm2, %ymm12
 149         vandpd    %ymm3, %ymm2, %ymm13
 150         vandpd    %ymm9, %ymm2, %ymm4
 151         vandnpd   %ymm3, %ymm2, %ymm5
 152         vorpd     %ymm13, %ymm12, %ymm6
 153         vorpd     %ymm5, %ymm4, %ymm7
 154 
 155 /* d) Divide R = P / Q; */
 156         vdivpd    %ymm7, %ymm6, %ymm8
 157 
 158 /* Large values check */
 159         vcmpnle_uqpd _dReductionRangeVal+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm1, %ymm14
 160         vmovmskpd %ymm14, %eax
 161 
 162 /*
 163  * 3) Destination sign setting
 164  * a) Set shifted destination sign using XOR operation:
 165  * R = XOR( R, S );
 166  */
 167         vxorpd    %ymm0, %ymm8, %ymm0
 168         testl     %eax, %eax
 169 
 170 /* Go to auxilary branch */
 171         jne       L(AUX_BRANCH)
 172                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 r9d ymm0 ymm1 ymm14 ymm15
 173 
 174 /* Return from auxilary branch
 175  * for out of main path inputs
 176  */
 177 
 178 L(AUX_BRANCH_RETURN):
 179         testl     %r9d, %r9d
 180 
 181 /* Go to special inputs processing branch */
 182         jne       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH)
 183                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 r9d ymm0 ymm15
 184 
 185 /* Restore registers
 186  * and exit the function
 187  */
 188 
 189 L(EXIT):
 190         movq      %rbp, %rsp
 191         popq      %rbp
 192         cfi_def_cfa(7, 8)
 193         cfi_restore(6)
 194         ret
 195         cfi_def_cfa(6, 16)
 196         cfi_offset(6, -16)
 197 
 198 /* Branch to process
 199  * special inputs
 200  */
 201 
 202 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_BRANCH):
 203         vmovupd   %ymm15, 32(%rsp)
 204         vmovupd   %ymm0, 64(%rsp)
 205                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 r9d ymm0
 206 
 207         xorl      %eax, %eax
 208                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 eax r9d
 209 
 210         vzeroupper
 211         movq      %r12, 16(%rsp)
 212         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r12 (r12) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -80; DW_OP_plus)  */
 213         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0c, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xb0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 214         movl      %eax, %r12d
 215         movq      %r13, 8(%rsp)
 216         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r13 (r13) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -88; DW_OP_plus)  */
 217         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0d, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xa8, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 218         movl      %r9d, %r13d
 219         movq      %r14, (%rsp)
 220         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r14 (r14) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -96; DW_OP_plus)  */
 221         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0e, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xa0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 222                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 223 
 224 /* Range mask
 225  * bits check
 226  */
 227 
 228 L(RANGEMASK_CHECK):
 229         btl       %r12d, %r13d
 230 
 231 /* Call scalar math function */
 232         jc        L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL)
 233                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 234 
 235 /* Special inputs
 236  * processing loop
 237  */
 238 
 239 L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP):
 240         incl      %r12d
 241         cmpl      $4, %r12d
 242 
 243 /* Check bits in range mask */
 244         jl        L(RANGEMASK_CHECK)
 245                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 246 
 247         movq      16(%rsp), %r12
 248         cfi_restore(12)
 249         movq      8(%rsp), %r13
 250         cfi_restore(13)
 251         movq      (%rsp), %r14
 252         cfi_restore(14)
 253         vmovupd   64(%rsp), %ymm0
 254 
 255 /* Go to exit */
 256         jmp       L(EXIT)
 257         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r12 (r12) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -80; DW_OP_plus)  */
 258         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0c, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xb0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 259         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r13 (r13) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -88; DW_OP_plus)  */
 260         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0d, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xa8, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 261         /*  DW_CFA_expression: r14 (r14) (DW_OP_lit8; DW_OP_minus; DW_OP_const4s: -32; DW_OP_and; DW_OP_const4s: -96; DW_OP_plus)  */
 262         .cfi_escape 0x10, 0x0e, 0x0e, 0x38, 0x1c, 0x0d, 0xe0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x1a, 0x0d, 0xa0, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0x22
 263                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 ymm0
 264 
 265 /* Scalar math fucntion call
 266  * to process special input
 267  */
 268 
 269 L(SCALAR_MATH_CALL):
 270         movl      %r12d, %r14d
 271         movsd     32(%rsp,%r14,8), %xmm0
 272         call      tan@PLT
 273                                 # LOE rbx r14 r15 r12d r13d xmm0
 274 
 275         movsd     %xmm0, 64(%rsp,%r14,8)
 276 
 277 /* Process special inputs in loop */
 278         jmp       L(SPECIAL_VALUES_LOOP)
 279         cfi_restore(12)
 280         cfi_restore(13)
 281         cfi_restore(14)
 282                                 # LOE rbx r15 r12d r13d
 283 
 284 /* Auxilary branch
 285  * for out of main path inputs
 286  */
 287 
 288 L(AUX_BRANCH):
 289         vpand     .FLT_17(%rip), %ymm15, %ymm4
 290 
 291 /*
 292  * Get the (2^a / 2pi) mod 1 values from the table.
 293  * Because doesn't have L-type gather, we need a trivial cast
 294  */
 295         lea       __svml_dtan_reduction_data_internal(%rip), %r8
 296         vmovupd   _dRangeVal+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %ymm6
 297         vmovupd   %ymm0, (%rsp)
 298         vpsrlq    $52, %ymm4, %ymm13
 299         vandpd    %ymm1, %ymm6, %ymm12
 300         vcmpeqpd  %ymm6, %ymm12, %ymm7
 301         vmovmskpd %ymm7, %r9d
 302         vextractf128 $1, %ymm13, %xmm8
 303         vmovd     %xmm13, %r10d
 304         vmovd     %xmm8, %edx
 305         vpextrd   $2, %xmm13, %r11d
 306         lea       (%r10,%r10,2), %edi
 307         vpextrd   $2, %xmm8, %eax
 308         lea       (%rdx,%rdx,2), %ecx
 309         shll      $3, %edi
 310         shll      $3, %ecx
 311 
 312 /*
 313  * Also get the significand as an integer
 314  * NB: adding in the integer bit is wrong for denorms!
 315  * To make this work for denorms we should do something slightly different
 316  */
 317         vpand     .FLT_18(%rip), %ymm15, %ymm13
 318         lea       (%r11,%r11,2), %esi
 319         vmovq     (%rdi,%r8), %xmm10
 320         vmovq     (%rcx,%r8), %xmm5
 321         vmovq     8(%rdi,%r8), %xmm3
 322         shll      $3, %esi
 323         lea       (%rax,%rax,2), %r10d
 324         shll      $3, %r10d
 325         vmovhpd   (%rsi,%r8), %xmm10, %xmm9
 326         vmovhpd   (%r10,%r8), %xmm5, %xmm12
 327         vpaddq    .FLT_19(%rip), %ymm13, %ymm8
 328         vmovq     16(%rdi,%r8), %xmm1
 329         vmovq     8(%rcx,%r8), %xmm7
 330         vmovq     16(%rcx,%r8), %xmm11
 331         vmovhpd   8(%rsi,%r8), %xmm3, %xmm6
 332 
 333 /*  Load constants (not all needed at once)  */
 334         lea       _dCoeffs+96+__svml_dtan_data_internal(%rip), %rcx
 335         vmovhpd   16(%rsi,%r8), %xmm1, %xmm4
 336         vmovhpd   8(%r10,%r8), %xmm7, %xmm2
 337         vmovhpd   16(%r10,%r8), %xmm11, %xmm0
 338         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm12, %ymm9, %ymm10
 339 
 340 /*
 341  * Break the P_xxx and m into 32-bit chunks ready for
 342  * the long multiplication via 32x32->64 multiplications
 343  */
 344         vmovdqu   .FLT_20(%rip), %ymm12
 345         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm10, %ymm7
 346         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm10, %ymm10
 347         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm2, %ymm6, %ymm9
 348         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm0, %ymm4, %ymm11
 349         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm9, %ymm4
 350         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm9, %ymm2
 351         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm8, %ymm9
 352         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm11, %ymm5
 353         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm11, %ymm0
 354         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm8, %ymm6
 355         vpmuludq  %ymm5, %ymm9, %ymm11
 356         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm11, %ymm5
 357         vpmuludq  %ymm0, %ymm9, %ymm11
 358         vpmuludq  %ymm0, %ymm6, %ymm0
 359         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm0, %ymm0
 360         vpmuludq  %ymm2, %ymm6, %ymm1
 361         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm1, %ymm13
 362         vpaddq    %ymm0, %ymm11, %ymm11
 363         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm1, %ymm1
 364         vpaddq    %ymm11, %ymm13, %ymm13
 365         vpmuludq  %ymm4, %ymm6, %ymm3
 366         vpmuludq  %ymm2, %ymm9, %ymm2
 367         vpaddq    %ymm13, %ymm5, %ymm11
 368         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm3, %ymm5
 369         vpaddq    %ymm1, %ymm2, %ymm2
 370         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm3, %ymm3
 371         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm11, %ymm13
 372         vpaddq    %ymm2, %ymm5, %ymm5
 373         vpmuludq  %ymm7, %ymm6, %ymm8
 374         vpaddq    %ymm5, %ymm13, %ymm5
 375         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm8, %ymm1
 376         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm5, %ymm0
 377         vpsllq    $32, %ymm5, %ymm5
 378         vpmuludq  %ymm4, %ymm9, %ymm13
 379         vpaddq    %ymm3, %ymm13, %ymm13
 380         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm8, %ymm4
 381         vpaddq    %ymm13, %ymm1, %ymm3
 382         vpmuludq  %ymm10, %ymm6, %ymm6
 383 
 384 /* Now do the big multiplication and carry propagation */
 385         vpmuludq  %ymm7, %ymm9, %ymm7
 386         vpaddq    %ymm3, %ymm0, %ymm2
 387         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm6, %ymm10
 388         vpaddq    %ymm4, %ymm7, %ymm9
 389         vpsrlq    $32, %ymm2, %ymm13
 390         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm2, %ymm6
 391         vpaddq    %ymm9, %ymm10, %ymm8
 392 
 393 /* Assemble reduced argument from the pieces */
 394         vpand     %ymm12, %ymm11, %ymm12
 395         vpaddq    %ymm8, %ymm13, %ymm13
 396 
 397 /*
 398  * We want to incorporate the original sign now too.
 399  * Do it here for convenience in getting the right N value,
 400  * though we could wait right to the end if we were prepared
 401  * to modify the sign of N later too.
 402  * So get the appropriate sign mask now (or sooner).
 403  */
 404         vpand     .FLT_21(%rip), %ymm15, %ymm8
 405         vpaddq    %ymm12, %ymm5, %ymm9
 406 
 407 /*
 408  * Now round at the 2^-9 bit position for reduction mod pi/2^8
 409  * instead of the original 2pi (but still with the same 2pi scaling).
 410  * Use a shifter of 2^43 + 2^42.
 411  * The N we get is our final version; it has an offset of
 412  * 2^9 because of the implicit integer bit, and anyway for negative
 413  * starting value it's a 2s complement thing. But we need to mask
 414  * off the exponent part anyway so it's fine.
 415  */
 416         vmovupd   .FLT_23(%rip), %ymm5
 417         vpsllq    $32, %ymm13, %ymm3
 418 
 419 /*
 420  * Create floating-point high part, implicitly adding integer bit 1
 421  * Incorporate overall sign at this stage too.
 422  */
 423         vpxor     .FLT_22(%rip), %ymm8, %ymm10
 424 
 425 /*
 426  * Create floating-point low and medium parts, respectively
 427  * lo_23, ... lo_0, 0, ..., 0
 428  * hi_11, ... hi_0, lo_63, ..., lo_24
 429  * then subtract off the implicitly added integer bits,
 430  * 2^-104 and 2^-52, respectively.
 431  * Put the original sign into all of them at this stage.
 432  */
 433         vpxor     .FLT_24(%rip), %ymm8, %ymm4
 434         vpand     .FLT_25(%rip), %ymm9, %ymm7
 435         vpaddq    %ymm6, %ymm3, %ymm3
 436         vpsrlq    $24, %ymm9, %ymm9
 437         vpsllq    $28, %ymm7, %ymm2
 438         vpsrlq    $12, %ymm3, %ymm13
 439         vpor      %ymm4, %ymm2, %ymm1
 440         vpor      %ymm10, %ymm13, %ymm12
 441         vsubpd    %ymm4, %ymm1, %ymm13
 442         vaddpd    %ymm5, %ymm12, %ymm10
 443         vsubpd    %ymm5, %ymm10, %ymm6
 444         vpxor     .FLT_26(%rip), %ymm8, %ymm5
 445         vpand     .FLT_27(%rip), %ymm3, %ymm8
 446         vsubpd    %ymm6, %ymm12, %ymm0
 447         vpsllq    $40, %ymm8, %ymm3
 448         vpor      %ymm9, %ymm3, %ymm11
 449 
 450 /*
 451  * If the magnitude of the input is <= 2^-20, then
 452  * just pass through the input, since no reduction will be needed and
 453  * the main path will only work accurately if the reduced argument is
 454  * about >= 2^-70 (which it is for all large pi multiples)
 455  */
 456         vmovupd   .FLT_31(%rip), %ymm3
 457         vpor      %ymm5, %ymm11, %ymm9
 458         vsubpd    %ymm5, %ymm9, %ymm8
 459 
 460 /* Now add them up into 2 reasonably aligned pieces */
 461         vaddpd    %ymm8, %ymm0, %ymm12
 462         vsubpd    %ymm12, %ymm0, %ymm0
 463         vaddpd    %ymm0, %ymm8, %ymm9
 464 
 465 /*
 466  * Now multiply those numbers all by 2 pi, reasonably accurately.
 467  * (RHi + RLo) * (pi_lead + pi_trail) ~=
 468  * RHi * pi_lead + (RHi * pi_trail + RLo * pi_lead)
 469  */
 470         vmovupd   .FLT_28(%rip), %ymm8
 471         vaddpd    %ymm9, %ymm13, %ymm11
 472         vmulpd    %ymm12, %ymm8, %ymm7
 473         vmovapd   %ymm8, %ymm13
 474         vfmsub213pd %ymm7, %ymm12, %ymm13
 475 
 476 /* Grab our final N value as an integer, appropriately masked mod 2^9 */
 477         vandps    .FLT_32(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm10
 478 
 479 /*
 480  * Argument reduction is now finished: x = n * pi/256 + r
 481  * where n = lIndex and r = dZ
 482  * But we have n modulo 512, needed for sin/cos with period 2pi
 483  * but we want it modulo 256 since tan has period pi.
 484  */
 485         vandps    .FLT_33(%rip), %ymm10, %ymm10
 486         vandpd    .FLT_30(%rip), %ymm15, %ymm5
 487         vcmpgt_oqpd %ymm3, %ymm5, %ymm4
 488         vcmple_oqpd %ymm3, %ymm5, %ymm6
 489         vfmadd132pd .FLT_29(%rip), %ymm13, %ymm12
 490         vfmadd213pd %ymm12, %ymm8, %ymm11
 491         vandpd    %ymm15, %ymm6, %ymm2
 492         vandpd    %ymm7, %ymm4, %ymm1
 493         vorpd     %ymm1, %ymm2, %ymm0
 494         vandpd    %ymm11, %ymm4, %ymm13
 495 
 496 /*
 497  * The output is _VRES_Z (high) + _VRES_E (low), and the integer part is _VRES_IND
 498  * Simply absorb E into Z instead of keeping a 2-part result.
 499  */
 500         vaddpd    %ymm13, %ymm0, %ymm13
 501         vextractf128 $1, %ymm10, %xmm5
 502         vmovd     %xmm10, %edi
 503         vmovd     %xmm5, %r11d
 504         imull     $104, %edi, %edx
 505         imull     $104, %r11d, %esi
 506         vmovq     -96(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm9
 507         vmovq     -80(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm6
 508         vpextrd   $2, %xmm10, %r8d
 509         vpextrd   $2, %xmm5, %edi
 510         imull     $104, %r8d, %eax
 511         imull     $104, %edi, %r8d
 512         vmovq     -96(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm12
 513         vmovq     -72(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm4
 514         vmovq     -80(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm2
 515         vmovhpd   -96(%rax,%rcx), %xmm9, %xmm8
 516         vmovhpd   -96(%r8,%rcx), %xmm12, %xmm3
 517         vmovq     -56(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm9
 518         vmovq     -72(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm0
 519         vmovq     -56(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm5
 520         vmovhpd   -80(%rax,%rcx), %xmm6, %xmm7
 521         vmovhpd   -72(%rax,%rcx), %xmm4, %xmm11
 522         vmovhpd   -80(%r8,%rcx), %xmm2, %xmm1
 523         vmovhpd   -72(%r8,%rcx), %xmm0, %xmm10
 524         vmovq     -48(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm6
 525         vmovq     -48(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm0
 526         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm3, %ymm8, %ymm12
 527         vmovhpd   -56(%rax,%rcx), %xmm9, %xmm8
 528         vmovhpd   -56(%r8,%rcx), %xmm5, %xmm3
 529         vmovq     -40(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm9
 530         vmovq     -40(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm5
 531         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm1, %ymm7, %ymm2
 532         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm10, %ymm11, %ymm1
 533         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm3, %ymm8, %ymm4
 534         vmovhpd   -48(%rax,%rcx), %xmm6, %xmm7
 535         vmovhpd   -40(%rax,%rcx), %xmm9, %xmm8
 536         vmovq     -32(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm11
 537         vmovhpd   -48(%r8,%rcx), %xmm0, %xmm10
 538         vmovhpd   -40(%r8,%rcx), %xmm5, %xmm6
 539         vmovq     -32(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm9
 540         vmovhpd   -32(%rax,%rcx), %xmm11, %xmm0
 541         vmovq     -24(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm11
 542         vmovq     -24(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm5
 543 
 544 /*
 545  *  Sum of dominant component(s)
 546  * Compute C0_hi + C1_hi * Z + Recip_hi = H4
 547  * H2 = C0_hi + C1_hi * Z (exact since C1_hi is 1 bit)
 548  */
 549         vfmadd213pd %ymm1, %ymm13, %ymm4
 550 
 551 /*
 552  *  Higher polynomial terms
 553  * Stage 1 (with unlimited parallelism)
 554  * Z2 = Z^2
 555  */
 556         vmulpd    %ymm13, %ymm13, %ymm1
 557         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm10, %ymm7, %ymm3
 558         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm6, %ymm8, %ymm10
 559         vmovhpd   -32(%r8,%rcx), %xmm9, %xmm8
 560         vmovhpd   -24(%r8,%rcx), %xmm11, %xmm9
 561         vmovq     -16(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm11
 562         vmovhpd   -24(%rax,%rcx), %xmm5, %xmm7
 563 
 564 /* P4 = C1_lo + C2 * Z */
 565         vfmadd213pd %ymm3, %ymm13, %ymm10
 566         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm8, %ymm0, %ymm6
 567         vmovq     -16(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm8
 568         vmovhpd   -16(%rax,%rcx), %xmm8, %xmm5
 569         vmovhpd   -16(%r8,%rcx), %xmm11, %xmm0
 570         vmovq     -8(%rdx,%rcx), %xmm8
 571         vmovq     -8(%rsi,%rcx), %xmm11
 572         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm9, %ymm7, %ymm9
 573         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm0, %ymm5, %ymm7
 574         vmovhpd   -8(%rax,%rcx), %xmm8, %xmm5
 575         vmovhpd   -8(%r8,%rcx), %xmm11, %xmm0
 576 
 577 /* P5 = C3 + C4 * Z */
 578         vfmadd213pd %ymm6, %ymm13, %ymm9
 579 
 580 /* P10 = C1_lo + C2 * Z + C3 * Z^2 + C4 * Z^3 */
 581         vfmadd213pd %ymm10, %ymm1, %ymm9
 582         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm0, %ymm5, %ymm8
 583         vmovq     (%rdx,%rcx), %xmm5
 584         vmovq     (%rsi,%rcx), %xmm0
 585         vmovhpd   (%rax,%rcx), %xmm5, %xmm11
 586         vmovhpd   (%r8,%rcx), %xmm0, %xmm5
 587 
 588 /* P6 = C5 + C6 * Z */
 589         vfmadd213pd %ymm7, %ymm13, %ymm8
 590         vinsertf128 $1, %xmm5, %ymm11, %ymm5
 591 
 592 /*
 593  *  Compute reciprocal component
 594  * Construct a separate reduced argument modulo pi near pi/2 multiples.
 595  * i.e. (pi/2 - x) mod pi, simply by subtracting the reduced argument
 596  * from an accurate B_hi = (128 - n) pi/256.
 597  */
 598         vsubpd    %ymm13, %ymm12, %ymm11
 599 
 600 /* P9 = C5 + C6 * Z + C7 * Z^2 */
 601         vfmadd213pd %ymm8, %ymm1, %ymm5
 602 
 603 /* Now compute an approximate reciprocal to mix into the computation. */
 604         vcvtpd2ps %ymm11, %xmm12
 605         vrcpps    %xmm12, %xmm12
 606         vcvtps2pd %xmm12, %ymm0
 607 
 608 /*
 609  * Now compute the error dEr where dRecip_hi = (1/R_full) * (1 - dEr)
 610  * so that we can compensate for it.
 611  */
 612         vfnmadd213pd .FLT_34(%rip), %ymm0, %ymm11
 613 
 614 /*
 615  * Get a working-precision reciprocal 1/dR_full
 616  * using a fourth-order polynomial approximation
 617  * R + (E*R) * (1 + E) * (1 + E^2)
 618  */
 619         vmulpd    %ymm11, %ymm11, %ymm12
 620         vfmadd213pd %ymm11, %ymm11, %ymm11
 621         vfmadd213pd %ymm0, %ymm0, %ymm12
 622         vfmadd213pd %ymm0, %ymm11, %ymm12
 623 
 624 /*
 625  *
 626  * End of large arguments path
 627  *
 628  * Merge results from main and large paths:
 629  */
 630         vmovupd   (%rsp), %ymm0
 631 
 632 /*
 633  * dRecip_hi is only used when dTau is one (cotangent path)
 634  * H4 = C0_hi + C1_hi * Z + Recip_hi
 635  */
 636         vfmadd213pd %ymm4, %ymm2, %ymm12
 637 
 638 /*
 639  * Stage 2 (with unlimited parallelism)
 640  * Z4 = Z^4
 641  */
 642         vmulpd    %ymm1, %ymm1, %ymm2
 643 
 644 /*
 645  * Stage 3 (with unlimited parallelism)
 646  * P12 = C1_lo + C2 * Z + ... + C7 * Z^6
 647  */
 648         vfmadd213pd %ymm9, %ymm2, %ymm5
 649 
 650 /* And now the very final summation */
 651         vfmadd213pd %ymm12, %ymm13, %ymm5
 652         vblendvpd %ymm14, %ymm5, %ymm0, %ymm0
 653 
 654 /* Return to main vector processing path */
 655         jmp       L(AUX_BRANCH_RETURN)
 656                                 # LOE rbx r12 r13 r14 r15 r9d ymm0 ymm15
 657 END(_ZGVdN4v_tan_avx2)
 658

 660         .align 32
